It is the third  and completes the trilogy of  sustainable city policies, environmental, social and economic. The ESS process has been both creative and extensive. The Draft ESS report represents the work of hundreds of Burnaby representatives and stakeholders  citizens, business representatives, and non-profit organizations. Together, we have developed a draft plan intended to provide clear direction to staff and information for the public on priorities for City action.  Before the ESS is submitted to Council for adoption, the City is checking in with you to see if we're on the right track, as part of our third and final phase of ESS public consultation. </p>\n<p>For more information on the Draft ESS and the ESS process, please visit <a href=\"/City-Services/Policies--Projects---Initiatives/Environment/Environmental-Sustainability-Strategy/Public-Consultation.html\" title=\"Public Consultation\">www.burnaby.ca/ess-input</a>. We will welcome your input here and at public events throughout the city.</p>\n<p><strong>Mayor Derek Corrigan</strong></p></div>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"secondarypromos\"><ul>\n    <li class=\"first\"><img width=\"150\" height=\"110\" alt=\"Photograph\" src=\"/Assets/New+Things+To+Do/Be+Active+Programs+new/Leisure+Guide+-+City+Home+Page+Image.jpg\">\n    <h3>Live an Active and Healthy Lifestyle!</h3>\n    <p>Flip through the Fall / Winter Leisure Guide and be active Burnaby!\n    <br>\n    <a href=\"/Things-To-Do/Be-Active-Programs/Leisure-Guide.html\" title=\"View More\"><strong>View more </strong></a></p>\n    </li>\n    <li>\n    <img alt=\"Business Watch logo\" business communities and the Burnaby RCMP providing tools and resources to help reduce and prevent crime in Burnaby.<br>\n    <a Board of Trade (BBOT) works to attract and retain new business and create a favourable business environment to stimulate economic growth in the community.<br>\n    <a
